			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Deaths in 2017</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>This is a chronology of <b>deaths in 2017</b>. Names are reported under the date of death. Names under each date are reported in alphabetical order by surname or pseudonym.</p>
<p>A typical entry reports information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship at birth, subsequent <a href="/wiki/Nationality" title="Nationality">nationality</a> (if applicable), what subject was noted for, cause of death (if known), and reference.</li>
</ul>
<div style="clear: right; margin-bottom: .5em; float: right; padding: .5em 0 .8em 1.4em; background: none; width: auto;">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="26">26</span></h3>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="25">25</span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eman_Ahmed_Abd_El_Aty" title="Eman Ahmed Abd El Aty">Eman Ahmed Abd El Aty</a>, 37, Egyptian woman, <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_heaviest_people" title="List of the heaviest people">world's heaviest</a>, kidney failure and intestinal shock.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anatoly_Gromyko" title="Anatoly Gromyko">Anatoly Gromyko</a>, 85, Soviet and Russian scientist and diplomat<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aneurin_Jones" title="Aneurin Jones">Aneurin Jones</a>, 87, Welsh painter.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bobby_Knutt" title="Bobby Knutt">Bobby Knutt</a>, 71, British actor and comedian (<i><a href="/wiki/Coronation_Street" title="Coronation Street">Coronation Street</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Benidorm_(TV_series)" title="Benidorm (TV series)">Benidorm</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Emmerdale" title="Emmerdale">Emmerdale</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Mainse" title="David Mainse">David Mainse</a>, 81, Canadian televangelist (<i><a href="/wiki/100_Huntley_Street" title="100 Huntley Street">100 Huntley Street</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Leonard_Mashako_Mamba" title="Leonard Mashako Mamba">Leonard Mashako Mamba</a>, 65–66, Congolese politician, <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Public_Health_(Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo)" title="Ministry of Public Health (Democratic Republic of the Congo)">Minister of Public Health</a> (1997–2001) and Minister of Higher Education and Universities (2008–2012).<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arun_Sadhu" title="Arun Sadhu">Arun Sadhu</a>, 76, Indian writer (<i><a href="/wiki/Sinhasan" title="Sinhasan">Sinhasan</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jan_T%C5%99%C3%ADska" title="Jan Tříska">Jan Tříska</a>, 80, Czech actor (<i><a href="/wiki/Andersonville_(film)" title="Andersonville (film)">Andersonville</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Karate_Kid_Part_III" title="The Karate Kid Part III">The Karate Kid Part III</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/2010_(film)" title="2010 (film)">2010</a></i>), fall.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="24">24</span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mar%C3%ADa_Julia_Alsogaray" title="María Julia Alsogaray">María Julia Alsogaray</a>, 74, Argentine politician, <a href="/wiki/Argentine_Chamber_of_Deputies" title="Argentine Chamber of Deputies">MP</a> for <a href="/wiki/City_of_Buenos_Aires" class="mw-redirect" title="City of Buenos Aires">City of Buenos Aires</a> (1985–1991) and Secretary of <a href="/wiki/Environment_of_Argentina" title="Environment of Argentina">Natural Resources and Sustainable Development</a> (1991–1999), pancreatic cancer.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Valery_Asapov" title="Valery Asapov">Valery Asapov</a>, 51, Russian army general, blast injury.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Washington_Benavides" title="Washington Benavides">Washington Benavides</a>, 87, Uruguayan poet, professor and musician.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barbara_Blaine" title="Barbara Blaine">Barbara Blaine</a>, 61, American humanitarian, founder of <a href="/wiki/Survivors_Network_of_those_Abused_by_Priests" title="Survivors Network of those Abused by Priests">SNAP</a>, heart disease.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nills_Campbell&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nills Campbell (page does not exist)">Nills Campbell</a>, 73, Guyanan journalist (<i><a href="/wiki/Stabroek_News" title="Stabroek News">Stabroek News</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gis%C3%A8le_Casadesus" title="Gisèle Casadesus">Gisèle Casadesus</a>, 103, French actress (<i><a href="/wiki/My_Afternoons_with_Margueritte" title="My Afternoons with Margueritte">My Afternoons with Margueritte</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=John_Gallop&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="John Gallop (page does not exist)">John Gallop</a>, 87, Australian judge.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Abdul_Majid_(actor)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Abdul Majid (actor) (page does not exist)">Abdul Majid</a>, 86, Indian actor and filmmaker, heart attack.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Orville_Lynn_Majors" title="Orville Lynn Majors">Orville Lynn Majors</a>, 56, American serial killer, heart failure.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Manuel_da_Silva_Martins" title="Manuel da Silva Martins">Manuel da Silva Martins</a>, 90, Portuguese Roman Catholic prelate, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Set%C3%BAbal" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Setúbal">Setúbal</a> (1975–1998).<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joseph_M._McDade" title="Joseph M. McDade">Joseph M. McDade</a>, 85, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">U.S. House of Representatives</a> for <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania%27s_10th_congressional_district" title="Pennsylvania's 10th congressional district">Pennsylvania's 10th</a> (1963–1999).<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kit_Reed" title="Kit Reed">Kit Reed</a>, 85, American science fiction and mystery writer, brain tumor.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Viktor_Tolmachev&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Viktor Tolmachev (page does not exist)">Viktor Tolmachev</a>, 78, Russian ice hockey player (<a href="/wiki/HC_CSKA_Moscow" title="HC CSKA Moscow">CSKA Moscow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union_national_ice_hockey_team" title="Soviet Union national ice hockey team">national team</a>), stabbed.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> (body discovered on this date)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="23">23</span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charles_Bradley_(singer)" title="Charles Bradley (singer)">Charles Bradley</a>, 68, American singer ("<a href="/wiki/Changes_(Black_Sabbath_song)" title="Changes (Black Sabbath song)">Changes</a>"), stomach cancer.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Loreto_Carbonell" title="Loreto Carbonell">Loreto Carbonell</a>, 84, Filipino basketball player, cardiac arrest.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dorothy_Eck" title="Dorothy Eck">Dorothy Eck</a>, 93, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/Montana_Senate" title="Montana Senate">Montana Senate</a> (1980–2000).<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Seth_Firkins" title="Seth Firkins">Seth Firkins</a>, 36, American audio engineer (<a href="/wiki/Future_(rapper)" title="Future (rapper)">Future</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a>, <a href="/wiki/Young_Thug" title="Young Thug">Young Thug</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_D._Phillips" title="Elizabeth D. Phillips">Elizabeth D. Phillips</a>, 72, American educator and academic administrator.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Tsisana_Tatishvili&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tsisana Tatishvili (page does not exist)">Tsisana Tatishvili</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://ka.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E1%83%AA%E1%83%98%E1%83%A1%E1%83%90%E1%83%9C%E1%83%90_%E1%83%A2%E1%83%90%E1%83%A2%E1%83%98%E1%83%A8%E1%83%95%E1%83%98%E1%83%9A%E1%83%98" class="extiw" title="ka:ცისანა ტატიშვილი">ka</a>)</span>, 79, Georgian opera singer, <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Artist_of_the_USSR" title="People's Artist of the USSR">People's Artist of the USSR</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Samuel_H._Young" title="Samuel H. Young">Samuel H. Young</a>, 94, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">U.S. House of Representatives</a> from <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a> (1973–1975).<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
</ul>

<ul>

<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lloyd_Watson_(journalist)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lloyd Watson (journalist) (page does not exist)">Lloyd Watson</a>, 91, American journalist (<i><a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Chronicle" title="San Francisco Chronicle">San Francisco Chronicle</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-351" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-351">[351]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Xiang_Shouzhi" title="Xiang Shouzhi">Xiang Shouzhi</a>, 99, Chinese general, commander of the <a href="/wiki/Nanjing_Military_Region" title="Nanjing Military Region">Nanjing Military Region</a> (1982–1990) and the <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Liberation_Army_Rocket_Force" title="People's Liberation Army Rocket Force">Second Artillery Corps</a> (1975–1977).<sup id="cite_ref-352" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-352">[352]</a></sup></li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Tony_Hakaoro" title="Tony Hakaoro">Tony Hakaoro</a>, Cook Islands broadcaster and radio talk show host (<i><a href="/wiki/Radio_Cook_Islands" title="Radio Cook Islands">Radio Cook Islands</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-364" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-364">[364]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Peadar_Lamb" title="Peadar Lamb">Peadar Lamb</a>, 87, Irish actor (<i><a href="/wiki/Jakers!_The_Adventures_of_Piggley_Winks" title="Jakers! Narozanick</a>, 96, American politician, mayor of <a href="/wiki/Englishtown,_New_Jersey" title="Englishtown, New Jersey">Englishtown, New Jersey</a> (1954–1966).<sup id="cite_ref-370" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-370">[370]</a></sup></li>
